    <script language="javascript">
        $(function () {

            // 判断浏览器是否支持 placeholder
            placeholderLoad();

            function placeholderLoad() {
                if (!placeholderSupport()) {
                    $('[placeholder]').focus(function () {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.val('');
                            input.removeClass('placeholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function () {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.addClass('placeholder');
                            input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
                        }
                    }).blur();
                }
                ;
            }

            function placeholderSupport() {
                return 'placeholder' in document.createElement('input');
            }
        });

        $(function () {
            
            $(".chosen-select").chosen({ disable_search_threshold: 100 });
            $(".QueryForm .ForTips").mouseenter(function (e) {
                $("#Tips").fadeIn("fast").show();
            });
            $(".QueryForm .ForTips").mouseleave(function (e) {
                $("#Tips").fadeOut("fast").hide();
            });
            $("#VerificationCode").click(function (e) {
                
                
                if ($("#Phone").val() == "") {
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('手机号不能为空！',
                        {
                            'type': 'error',
                            'title': '错误信息提示框'
                        });
                    return;
                }
                if (!$("#Phone").val().match(/^1\d{10}$/)) {
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('手机号格式错误！',
                        {
                            'type': 'error',
                            'title': '错误信息提示框'
                        });

                    return;
                }

                $.ajax({
                    url: "../Web/SendPhoneCode.ashx",
                    type: "Post",
                    data: { Phone: $("#Phone").val(), Prefix: $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase(), CarNumber: $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase(), CarCode: $('#txtCarCode').val(), CarDrive: $('#txtCarDrive').val(), Owner: '' },
                    async: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function (result) {

                        if (result.success == true) {

                            DelayCodeTime($("#VerificationCode"), 60);
                        
                            $.Zebra_Dialog('验证码已发送，请查收手机短信',
                                {
                                    'type': 'information',
                                    'title': '提示框'
                                });
             
                        }
                        else 
                        {
                        
                        
                            $.Zebra_Dialog(result.errMsg,
                                {
                                    'type': 'error',
                                    'title': '错误信息提示框'
                                });
                            return false;

                        }

                    }
                });
            });
            $(".ManualOrder").hide();
            $("#ManualBtn").click(function (e) {
                ShowManualForm();
            });
            $("#DropDownForm").click(function (e) {
                ShowManualForm();
            });
            $(".OrdersList li:odd").css("background-color", "#e2f2ff"); //改变偶数行背景色
        });
        function ShowManualForm() {
            var disable = $(".ManualOrder").css("display");
            if (disable == "none") {
                $(".ManualOrder").fadeIn("fast").show("fast");
                $("#DropDownForm").removeClass().addClass("up");
            } else {
                $(".ManualOrder").fadeOut("fast").hide("fast");
                $("#DropDownForm").removeClass().addClass("down");
            }
        }
        function DelayCodeTime(o, t) {//o为按钮的对象，t为时间
            if (t == 0) {
                o.removeAttr("disabled");
                o.removeClass("VerificationCodeDisabled").addClass("VerificationCode");
                o.text("获取验证码"); //改变按钮中value的值 
            } else {
                o.attr("disabled", true); //倒计时过程中禁止点击按钮
                o.addClass("VerificationCodeDisabled");
                o.text(t + " 秒"); //改变按钮中value的值 
                t--;
                setTimeout(function() {
                    DelayCodeTime(o, t); //循环调用 
                }, 1000);
            }
        }

        $(function() {
            
            // 判断浏览器是否支持 placeholder
            placeholderLoad();
            function placeholderLoad() {
                if (!placeholderSupport()) { 
                    $('[placeholder]').focus(function() {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.val('');
                            input.removeClass('placeholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function() {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.addClass('placeholder');
                            input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
                        }
                    }).blur();
                }; 
            }
            
            function placeholderSupport() {
                return 'placeholder' in document.createElement('input');
            }
            
            //根据对应的参数提示要输入的车架和发动机号长度
            var setCity = function (infor) {
                var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                var carPrefix = inforArray[0];
                var carEngineLen = inforArray[1];
                var carCarcodeLen = inforArray[2];
                var carOwnerLen = inforArray[3];
                var cityId = inforArray[4];
                
                $("#lblViolationCount").text("");
                $("#lblCarNumber").text("");
                $('#txtPrefix').val(carPrefix);
                $('#txtCarNumber').attr('maxLength', 7 - carPrefix.length);
                //$('#txtCarNumber').val('');
                //$('#txtCarDrive').val('');
                //$('#txtCarCode').val('');
                //$('#txtOwner').val('');
                if (carEngineLen > 0) {
                    $('#liCardrive').show();
                    if (carEngineLen == 99) {
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder', "完整发动机号"); 
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('maxLength', 99);     
                    } else {
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder', '发动机号后' + carEngineLen + '位'); 
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('maxLength', carEngineLen);
                    }
                } else {
                    $('#liCardrive').hide();
                    $('#txtCarDrive').val('');
                }
                if (carCarcodeLen > 0) {
                    $('#liCarFrame').show();
                    if (carCarcodeLen == 99) {
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder', "完整车架号");
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('maxLength', 99);
                    } else {
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder', '车架号后' + carCarcodeLen + '位');
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('carCarcodeLen', 99);
                    }
                } else {
                    $('#liCarFrame').hide();
                    $('#txtCarCode').val('');
                }
                //                if (carOwnerLen > 0) {
                //                    $('#liOwner').show();
                //                    if (carOwnerLen == 99) {
                //                        $('#lblCarOwner').text('完整车辆所有人');
                //                        $('#txtOwner').attr('maxLength', 99);
                //                    } else {
                //                        $('#lblCarOwner').text('车辆所有人后' + carOwnerLen + '位');
                //                        $('#txtOwner').attr('maxLength', carOwnerLen);
                //                    }
                //                } else {
                //                    $('#liOwner').hide();
                //                }
                placeholderLoad(); 
            }; 
            
            //初始化城市，车牌号

            function loadsCity() {
                // 先清空
                
                //                if ($("#Code_Hidden").val() == "code") {
                //                    alert("验证码错误！");
                //                } else {
                //                    document.getElementById('Phone_Li').style.display = "none";
                //                    document.getElementById('Code_Li').style.display = "none"; 
                //                }
                $("#City").empty();
                $("#prefix").empty();
                var index = 0;
                var url ;
                var carNumber ;
                var carPrefix ;
                var carCode ;
                var carEngine ;
                var province ;
                var city ;
                var phone;
                var code;
                if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                    url = $.url($.cookie('carCookie'));
                    carNumber = url.param('carNumber');
                    carPrefix = url.param('carPrefix');
                    carCode = url.param('carCode');
                    carEngine = url.param("carEngine");
                    province = url.param("province");
                    city = url.param("city");
                    phone = url.param("phone");
                    code = url.param("code");
                    $("#Province").val(province);
                    $("#Province").trigger("chosen:updated");
                } else {
                    var id = $("#txtProvince").val();
                    
                    if (id != "") {
                        $("#Province").val(id);
                        $("#Province").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    }
                    
                }
                for (var i = 0; i < InputsCondition.length; i++) {

                    var provinceId = $("#Province").val();
                    
                    if (InputsCondition[i].ProvinceID == provinceId) {
                      
                        for (var j = 0; j < InputsCondition[i].Cities.length; j++) {
                            
                            var citieName = '';
                            if (InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name.length > 5) {
                                citieName = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name.substring(0, 5);
                            } else {
                                citieName = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name;
                            }

                            var option = '<option  tag=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name + ' title=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + ' infor=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + ' proxyEnable=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].ProxyEnable + ' value=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + '>' + citieName + '</option>';
                            $("#City").append(option);
                            var prefixOption = '<option  tag=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name + ' title=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + ' infor=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + ' proxyEnable=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].ProxyEnable + ' value=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '>'+InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix+'</option>';
                            $("#prefix").append(prefixOption);
                            if (index == 0) {
                                var infor = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID;
                                setCity(infor);
                            }
                            index++;

                        }
                    }
                }
                
                $("#City").trigger("chosen:updated");
                $("#prefix").trigger("chosen:updated");
                
                if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                    
                    $("#City").val(city);
                    $("#prefix").val(carPrefix);
                    $("#City").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    $("#prefix").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    $('#txtCarNumber').val(carNumber.replace(carPrefix, '').toUpperCase());
                    $('#txtCarCode').val(carCode);
                    $('#txtCarDrive').val(carEngine);
                    $('#Phone').val(phone);
                }
                $('#txtPrefix').val($("#prefix").val());
                $("#txtProvince").val($("#Province").val());
                $("#txtCity").val($("#City").val());

            // chkAll全选事件
            $("#chkAll").bind("click", function () {
               
                if (document.getElementById("chkAll").checked) {

                       
                    var i = 0;
                    $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                        
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        if (inforArray[2] == '1') {
                            $(this).prop("checked", true);
                            i++;
                        }
                             
                    });
                    if (i == 0) {
                        $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);

                    allCheckbox();
                    
                } else {
                    $("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                    $("[name = chkAlls]:checkbox").prop('checked',false);
                    allCheckbox();
                }

            });
            
            // chkAll全选事件
            $("#chkAlls").bind("click", function () {
                
                if (document.getElementById("chkAlls").checked) {
                    
                    var i = 0;
                    $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                        
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        if (inforArray[2] == '1') {
                            $(this).prop("checked", true);
                            i++;
                        }
                             
                    });
                    if (i == 0) {
                        $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                        return;
                    }
                    //$("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop('checked',true);
                    $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop('checked',true);
                    allCheckbox();
                    
                } else {
                    $("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                    $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop('checked',false);
                    allCheckbox();
                }

            });
            
            //            $("#chkItem").bind("click", function () {

            //                allCheckbox();

            //            });

            var allCheckbox = function() {
                var sum = 0;
                var amount = 0;
                $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                    
                    if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        amount += parseFloat(inforArray[1]) + parseFloat(inforArray[3]);
                        sum++;

                    }
                });
                $("#Sum").html(sum); 
                $("#Amount").html(amount+".00");
            };

            

        });
        

        function checkInputsConditon () {
            var MinLen = 5;
            var carPrefix = $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
            var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
            var carCode = '';
            var carEngine = '';
            var carOwner = '';
            var $carCode = $('#txtCarCode');
            var $carEngine = $('#txtCarDrive');
            //var $carOwner = $('#txtOwner');
            

            if ($carCode.length > 0 && $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder')!=$carCode.val())
                carCode = $carCode.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            if ($carEngine.length > 0 && $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder')!=$carEngine.val())
                carEngine = $carEngine.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            //                if ($carOwner.length > 0)
            //                    carOwner = $carOwner.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');

            var conditions = $('option[infor ^=' + carPrefix + ']').attr('infor');
            if (conditions.length > 0) {
                var inforArray = conditions.split('*');
                var carEngineLen = inforArray[1] == 99 ? MinLen : inforArray[1];
                var carCarcodeLen = inforArray[2] == 99 ? MinLen : inforArray[2];
                //var carOwnerLen = inforArray[3] == 99 ? 2 : inforArray[3];                                //|| carOwnerLen > carOwner.length
                if (carNumber.length < 7 || carEngineLen > carEngine.length || carCarcodeLen > carCode.length ) {
                    return false;
                } else {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        };
            
        function addCookie () {
            var carPrefix = $('#txtPrefix').val().toUpperCase();//$('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
            var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
            var carCode = $('#txtCarCode').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var carEngine = $('#txtCarDrive').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            //  var carOwner = $('#txtOwner').val();
            var code = '';//$('#Code').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var phone = '';//$('#Phone').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var cookie = '';
            if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                var url = $.url($.cookie('carCookie'));
                if (url.param('carNumber') == carNumber) {
                    if (url.param('carCode') != null && url.param('carCode').length > carCode) {
                        carCode = url.param('carCode');
                    }
                    if (url.param('carEngine') != null && url.param('carEngine').length > carEngine) {
                        carEngine = url.param('carEngine');
                    }
                    //                    if (url.param('phone') != null) {
                    //                        phone = url.param('phone');
                    //                    }
                }
            }
            phone = phone.replace(/undefined/g, '');
            
            //$('#txtPrefix').val($("#prefix").val());
            //    $("#txtProvince").val($("#Province").val());
            //    $("#txtCity").val($("#City").val());    
            var province = $("#txtProvince").val();// $('#Province').val();
            var city = $("#txtCity").val();// $('#City').val();
            var cookieInfor = "?carPrefix=" + carPrefix + "&carNumber=" + carNumber + "&carCode=" + carCode + "&carEngine=" + carEngine + "&phone=" + phone + "&province=" + province + "&city=" + city+"&code="+code;
            // 方便读取参数,直接采用网站链接的形式 无其它特殊意义
            cookie = "http://www.cx580.com" + cookieInfor;
            //            cookie = cookie.replace(/undefined/g, '');
            $.cookie('carCookie', cookie, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
        };

        function submitBtn() {            
            if (checkInputsConditon()) {
                addCookie();
                //location.reload();
                window.location.href = '../Web/Query.aspx?action=queryPageBtn';
                return true;
            } else {
                $.Zebra_Dialog('您好！您输入的信息不符合要求，请按提示信息重新输入！',
                       {
                           'type': 'error',
                           'title': '错误信息提示框'
                       });
                return false;
            }
        };

        function onClickChk() {
            var sum = 0;
            var amount = 0;
            $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                    
                if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                    var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                    var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                    amount += parseFloat(inforArray[1]) + parseFloat(inforArray[3]);
                    sum++;

                }
            });
            $("#Sum").html(sum); 
            $("#Amount").html(amount+".00"); 
        }

        function CreateOrdersBtn() {               
            var id="";
            $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                    var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                    var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                    id += inforArray[0]+"*";
                }
            });
            if (id == "") {
                alert("请选择违章");
                return false;
            } else {
                
                var response = $.ajax({
                    url: "/CommonAshx/CheckLogin.ashx",
                    type: "POST",
                    async: false
                }).responseText;
                var data = jQuery.parseJSON(response);
                if (data.login) {
                    
                    id = id.substring(0, id.length - 1);
                    var carPrefix = $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
                    var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
                    var carCode = $('#txtCarCode').val();
                    var carDrive = $('#txtCarDrive').val();
                    
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('正在下单请稍后......',
                        {
                            'type': 'information',
                            'title': '提示框',
                            'buttons': ['关闭']
                        });

                    $.ajax({
                        url: "/Web/Admin/CreateOrder.ashx",
                        type: "Post",
                        data: { ids:id, carNumber: carNumber, carCode: carCode, carDrive: carDrive},
                        async: false,
                        dataType: "json",
                        success: function (result) {
                            if (result.status == "true") {
                                //
                                //                                $.Zebra_Dialog('创建订单成功！',
                                //                                    {
                                //                                        'type': 'information',
                                //                                        'title': '提示框',
                                //                                        'buttons': ['关闭']
                                //                                    
                                //                                    });
                                window.location = '/Web/Admin/Pay.aspx?Id=' + result.errorMsg;
                            }
                            else {
                                //                                $.Zebra_Dialog(result.errorMsg,
                                //                                    {
                                //                                        'type': 'error',
                                //                                        'title': '错误信息提示框',
                                //                                        'buttons':  ['关闭'],
                                //                                        'onClose':  function() {
                                //                                            this.close();
                                //                                        }
                                //                                    });

                                //                                window.location = '/Web/Query.aspx';
								$(".ZebraDialogOverlay").remove();
                                $(".ZebraDialog").remove();
                                alert(result.errorMsg);
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    });

                } else {
                    QuickLoginMethod();
                }                      
            }    
        };
    </script>

    <script>
        $(function () {
            //IsLogin();
            function IsLogin() {

                var isLogin = $("#IsLogin").val();
                
                if (isLogin == 1) {
                    $(".OrdersList").css({"display":"none"});
                    $(".Settle").css({"display":"none"});
                    QuickLoginMethod();
                }
                else
                {
                    $(".OrdersList").css({"display":"block"});
                    $(".Settle").css({"display":"block"});
                }
            }
        });
        //快捷登陆
        function CodeCickLogin(objid) {
            objid.src = '/CommonAshx/GenerateValImge.ashx?flag=' + new Date();
            document.getElementById("PicCode").value = "";
            document.getElementById("PicCode").focus();
        }
    </script>

        function setHomePage() {
            if (document.all) {
                document.body.style.behavior = 'url(#default#homepage)';
                document.body.setHomePage("http://www.cx580.com");
            } else if (window.sidebar) {
                if (window.netscape) {
                    try {
                        window.netscape.security.PrivilegeManager
                            .enablePrivilege("UniversalXPConnect");
                    } catch (e) {
                        alert("此操作被游览器拒绝！");
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    <script src="/Web/scripts/zebra_dialog.js" type="text/javascript"></script>

    <script language="javascript">
        $(function () {

            // 判断浏览器是否支持 placeholder
            placeholderLoad();

            function placeholderLoad() {
                if (!placeholderSupport()) {
                    $('[placeholder]').focus(function () {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.val('');
                            input.removeClass('placeholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function () {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.addClass('placeholder');
                            input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
                        }
                    }).blur();
                }
                ;
            }

            function placeholderSupport() {
                return 'placeholder' in document.createElement('input');
            }
        });

        $(function () {
            
            $(".chosen-select").chosen({ disable_search_threshold: 100 });
            $(".QueryForm .ForTips").mouseenter(function (e) {
                $("#Tips").fadeIn("fast").show();
            });
            $(".QueryForm .ForTips").mouseleave(function (e) {
                $("#Tips").fadeOut("fast").hide();
            });
            $("#VerificationCode").click(function (e) {
                
                
                if ($("#Phone").val() == "") {
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('手机号不能为空！',
                        {
                            'type': 'error',
                            'title': '错误信息提示框'
                        });
                    return;
                }
                if (!$("#Phone").val().match(/^1\d{10}$/)) {
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('手机号格式错误！',
                        {
                            'type': 'error',
                            'title': '错误信息提示框'
                        });

                    return;
                }

                $.ajax({
                    url: "../Web/SendPhoneCode.ashx",
                    type: "Post",
                    data: { Phone: $("#Phone").val(), Prefix: $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase(), CarNumber: $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase(), CarCode: $('#txtCarCode').val(), CarDrive: $('#txtCarDrive').val(), Owner: '' },
                    async: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function (result) {

                        if (result.success == true) {

                            DelayCodeTime($("#VerificationCode"), 60);
                        
                            $.Zebra_Dialog('验证码已发送，请查收手机短信',
                                {
                                    'type': 'information',
                                    'title': '提示框'
                                });
             
                        }
                        else 
                        {
                        
                        
                            $.Zebra_Dialog(result.errMsg,
                                {
                                    'type': 'error',
                                    'title': '错误信息提示框'
                                });
                            return false;

                        }

                    }
                });
            });
            $(".ManualOrder").hide();
            $("#ManualBtn").click(function (e) {
                ShowManualForm();
            });
            $("#DropDownForm").click(function (e) {
                ShowManualForm();
            });
            $(".OrdersList li:odd").css("background-color", "#e2f2ff"); //改变偶数行背景色
        });
        function ShowManualForm() {
            var disable = $(".ManualOrder").css("display");
            if (disable == "none") {
                $(".ManualOrder").fadeIn("fast").show("fast");
                $("#DropDownForm").removeClass().addClass("up");
            } else {
                $(".ManualOrder").fadeOut("fast").hide("fast");
                $("#DropDownForm").removeClass().addClass("down");
            }
        }
        function DelayCodeTime(o, t) {//o为按钮的对象，t为时间
            if (t == 0) {
                o.removeAttr("disabled");
                o.removeClass("VerificationCodeDisabled").addClass("VerificationCode");
                o.text("获取验证码"); //改变按钮中value的值 
            } else {
                o.attr("disabled", true); //倒计时过程中禁止点击按钮
                o.addClass("VerificationCodeDisabled");
                o.text(t + " 秒"); //改变按钮中value的值 
                t--;
                setTimeout(function() {
                    DelayCodeTime(o, t); //循环调用 
                }, 1000);
            }

        $(function() {
            
            // 判断浏览器是否支持 placeholder
            placeholderLoad();
            function placeholderLoad() {
                if (!placeholderSupport()) { 
                    $('[placeholder]').focus(function() {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.val('');
                            input.removeClass('placeholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function() {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.addClass('placeholder');
                            input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
                        }
                    }).blur();
                }; 
            }
            
            function placeholderSupport() {
                return 'placeholder' in document.createElement('input');
            }
            
            //根据对应的参数提示要输入的车架和发动机号长度
            var setCity = function (infor) {
                var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                var carPrefix = inforArray[0];
                var carEngineLen = inforArray[1];
                var carCarcodeLen = inforArray[2];
                var carOwnerLen = inforArray[3];
                var cityId = inforArray[4];
                
                $("#lblViolationCount").text("");
                $("#lblCarNumber").text("");
                $('#txtPrefix').val(carPrefix);
                $('#txtCarNumber').attr('maxLength', 7 - carPrefix.length);
                //$('#txtCarNumber').val('');
                //$('#txtCarDrive').val('');
                //$('#txtCarCode').val('');
                //$('#txtOwner').val('');
                if (carEngineLen > 0) {
                    $('#liCardrive').show();
                    if (carEngineLen == 99) {
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder', "完整发动机号"); 
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('maxLength', 99);     
                    } else {
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder', '发动机号后' + carEngineLen + '位'); 
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('maxLength', carEngineLen);
                    }
                } else {
                    $('#liCardrive').hide();
                    $('#txtCarDrive').val('');
                }
                if (carCarcodeLen > 0) {
                    $('#liCarFrame').show();
                    if (carCarcodeLen == 99) {
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder', "完整车架号");
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('maxLength', 99);
                    } else {
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder', '车架号后' + carCarcodeLen + '位');
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('carCarcodeLen', 99);
                    }
                } else {
                    $('#liCarFrame').hide();
                    $('#txtCarCode').val('');
                }
                //                if (carOwnerLen > 0) {
                //                    $('#liOwner').show();
                //                    if (carOwnerLen == 99) {
                //                        $('#lblCarOwner').text('完整车辆所有人');
                //                        $('#txtOwner').attr('maxLength', 99);
                //                    } else {
                //                        $('#lblCarOwner').text('车辆所有人后' + carOwnerLen + '位');
                //                        $('#txtOwner').attr('maxLength', carOwnerLen);
                //                    }
                //                } else {
                //                    $('#liOwner').hide();
                //                }
                placeholderLoad(); 
            }; 
            
            //初始化城市，车牌号

            function loadsCity() {
                // 先清空
                
                //                if ($("#Code_Hidden").val() == "code") {
                //                    alert("验证码错误！");
                //                } else {
                //                    document.getElementById('Phone_Li').style.display = "none";
                //                    document.getElementById('Code_Li').style.display = "none"; 
                //                }
                $("#City").empty();
                $("#prefix").empty();
                var index = 0;
                var url ;
                var carNumber ;
                var carPrefix ;
                var carCode ;
                var carEngine ;
                var province ;
                var city ;
                var phone;
                var code;
                if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                    url = $.url($.cookie('carCookie'));
                    carNumber = url.param('carNumber');
                    carPrefix = url.param('carPrefix');
                    carCode = url.param('carCode');
                    carEngine = url.param("carEngine");
                    province = url.param("province");
                    city = url.param("city");
                    phone = url.param("phone");
                    code = url.param("code");
                    $("#Province").val(province);
                    $("#Province").trigger("chosen:updated");
                } else {
                    var id = $("#txtProvince").val();
                    
                    if (id != "") {
                        $("#Province").val(id);
                        $("#Province").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    }
                    
                }
                for (var i = 0; i < InputsCondition.length; i++) {

                    var provinceId = $("#Province").val();
                    
                    if (InputsCondition[i].ProvinceID == provinceId) {
                      
                        for (var j = 0; j < InputsCondition[i].Cities.length; j++) {
                            
                            var citieName = '';
                            if (InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name.length > 5) {
                                citieName = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name.substring(0, 5);
                            } else {
                                citieName = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name;
                            }

                            var option = '<option  tag=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name + ' title=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + ' infor=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + ' proxyEnable=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].ProxyEnable + ' value=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + '>' + citieName + '</option>';
                            $("#City").append(option);
                            var prefixOption = '<option  tag=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name + ' title=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + ' infor=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + ' proxyEnable=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].ProxyEnable + ' value=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '>'+InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix+'</option>';
                            $("#prefix").append(prefixOption);
                            if (index == 0) {
                                var infor = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID;
                                setCity(infor);
                            }
                            index++;

                        }
                    }
                }
                
                $("#City").trigger("chosen:updated");
                $("#prefix").trigger("chosen:updated");
                
                if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                    
                    $("#City").val(city);
                    $("#prefix").val(carPrefix);
                    $("#City").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    $("#prefix").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    $('#txtCarNumber').val(carNumber.replace(carPrefix, '').toUpperCase());
                    $('#txtCarCode').val(carCode);
                    $('#txtCarDrive').val(carEngine);
                    $('#Phone').val(phone);
                }
                $('#txtPrefix').val($("#prefix").val());
                $("#txtProvince").val($("#Province").val());
                $("#txtCity").val($("#City").val());

            // chkAll全选事件
            $("#chkAll").bind("click", function () {
               
                if (document.getElementById("chkAll").checked) {

                       
                    var i = 0;
                    $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                        
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        if (inforArray[2] == '1') {
                            $(this).prop("checked", true);
                            i++;
                        }
                             
                    });
                    if (i == 0) {
                        $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);

                    allCheckbox();
                    
                } else {
                    $("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                    $("[name = chkAlls]:checkbox").prop('checked',false);
                    allCheckbox();
                }

            });
            
            // chkAll全选事件
            $("#chkAlls").bind("click", function () {
                
                if (document.getElementById("chkAlls").checked) {
                    
                    var i = 0;
                    $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                        
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        if (inforArray[2] == '1') {
                            $(this).prop("checked", true);
                            i++;
                        }
                             
                    });
                    if (i == 0) {
                        $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                        return;
                    }
                    //$("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop('checked',true);
                    $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop('checked',true);
                    allCheckbox();
                    
                } else {
                    $("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                    $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop('checked',false);
                    allCheckbox();
                }

            });
            
            //            $("#chkItem").bind("click", function () {

            //                allCheckbox();

            //            });

            var allCheckbox = function() {
                var sum = 0;
                var amount = 0;
                $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                    
                    if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        amount += parseFloat(inforArray[1]) + parseFloat(inforArray[3]);
                        sum++;

                    }
                });
                $("#Sum").html(sum); 
                $("#Amount").html(amount+".00");
            };

            

        });
        

        function checkInputsConditon () {
            var MinLen = 5;
            var carPrefix = $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
            var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
            var carCode = '';
            var carEngine = '';
            var carOwner = '';
            var $carCode = $('#txtCarCode');
            var $carEngine = $('#txtCarDrive');
            //var $carOwner = $('#txtOwner');
            

            if ($carCode.length > 0 && $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder')!=$carCode.val())
                carCode = $carCode.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            if ($carEngine.length > 0 && $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder')!=$carEngine.val())
                carEngine = $carEngine.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            //                if ($carOwner.length > 0)
            //                    carOwner = $carOwner.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');

            var conditions = $('option[infor ^=' + carPrefix + ']').attr('infor');
            if (conditions.length > 0) {
                var inforArray = conditions.split('*');
                var carEngineLen = inforArray[1] == 99 ? MinLen : inforArray[1];
                var carCarcodeLen = inforArray[2] == 99 ? MinLen : inforArray[2];
                //var carOwnerLen = inforArray[3] == 99 ? 2 : inforArray[3];                                //|| carOwnerLen > carOwner.length
                if (carNumber.length < 7 || carEngineLen > carEngine.length || carCarcodeLen > carCode.length ) {
                    return false;
                } else {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        };
            
        function addCookie () {
            var carPrefix = $('#txtPrefix').val().toUpperCase();//$('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
            var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
            var carCode = $('#txtCarCode').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var carEngine = $('#txtCarDrive').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            //  var carOwner = $('#txtOwner').val();
            var code = '';//$('#Code').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var phone = '';//$('#Phone').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var cookie = '';
            if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                var url = $.url($.cookie('carCookie'));
                if (url.param('carNumber') == carNumber) {
                    if (url.param('carCode') != null && url.param('carCode').length > carCode) {
                        carCode = url.param('carCode');
                    }
                    if (url.param('carEngine') != null && url.param('carEngine').length > carEngine) {
                        carEngine = url.param('carEngine');
                    }
                    //                    if (url.param('phone') != null) {
                    //                        phone = url.param('phone');
                    //                    }
                }
            }
            phone = phone.replace(/undefined/g, '');
            
            //$('#txtPrefix').val($("#prefix").val());
            //    $("#txtProvince").val($("#Province").val());
            //    $("#txtCity").val($("#City").val());    
            var province = $("#txtProvince").val();// $('#Province').val();
            var city = $("#txtCity").val();// $('#City').val();
            var cookieInfor = "?carPrefix=" + carPrefix + "&carNumber=" + carNumber + "&carCode=" + carCode + "&carEngine=" + carEngine + "&phone=" + phone + "&province=" + province + "&city=" + city+"&code="+code;
            // 方便读取参数,直接采用网站链接的形式 无其它特殊意义
            cookie = "http://www.cx580.com" + cookieInfor;
            //            cookie = cookie.replace(/undefined/g, '');
            $.cookie('carCookie', cookie, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
        };

        function submitBtn() {            
            if (checkInputsConditon()) {
                addCookie();
                //location.reload();
                window.location.href = '../Web/Query.aspx?action=queryPageBtn';
                return true;
            } else {
                $.Zebra_Dialog('您好！您输入的信息不符合要求，请按提示信息重新输入！',
                       {
                           'type': 'error',
                           'title': '错误信息提示框'
                       });
                return false;
            }
        };

        function onClickChk() {
            var sum = 0;
            var amount = 0;
            $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                    
                if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                    var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                    var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                    amount += parseFloat(inforArray[1]) + parseFloat(inforArray[3]);
                    sum++;

                }
            });
            $("#Sum").html(sum); 
            $("#Amount").html(amount+".00"); 
        }

        function CreateOrdersBtn() {               
            var id="";
            $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                    var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                    var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                    id += inforArray[0]+"*";
                }
            });
            if (id == "") {
                alert("请选择违章");
                return false;
            } else {
                
                var response = $.ajax({
                    url: "/CommonAshx/CheckLogin.ashx",
                    type: "POST",
                    async: false
                }).responseText;
                var data = jQuery.parseJSON(response);
                if (data.login) {
                    
                    id = id.substring(0, id.length - 1);
                    var carPrefix = $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
                    var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
                    var carCode = $('#txtCarCode').val();
                    var carDrive = $('#txtCarDrive').val();
                    
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('正在下单请稍后......',
                        {
                            'type': 'information',
                            'title': '提示框',
                            'buttons': ['关闭']
                        });

                    $.ajax({
                        url: "/Web/Admin/CreateOrder.ashx",
                        type: "Post",
                        data: { ids:id, carNumber: carNumber, carCode: carCode, carDrive: carDrive},
                        async: false,
                        dataType: "json",
                        success: function (result) {
                            if (result.status == "true") {
                                //
                                //                                $.Zebra_Dialog('创建订单成功！',
                                //                                    {
                                //                                        'type': 'information',
                                //                                        'title': '提示框',
                                //                                        'buttons': ['关闭']
                                //                                    
                                //                                    });
                                window.location = '/Web/Admin/Pay.aspx?Id=' + result.errorMsg;
                            }
                            else {
                                //                                $.Zebra_Dialog(result.errorMsg,
                                //                                    {
                                //                                        'type': 'error',
                                //                                        'title': '错误信息提示框',
                                //                                        'buttons':  ['关闭'],
                                //                                        'onClose':  function() {
                                //                                            this.close();
                                //                                        }
                                //                                    });

                                //                                window.location = '/Web/Query.aspx';
								$(".ZebraDialogOverlay").remove();
                                $(".ZebraDialog").remove();
                                alert(result.errorMsg);
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    });

                } else {
                    QuickLoginMethod();
                }                      
            }    
        };
    </script>

    <script>
        $(function () {
            //IsLogin();
            function IsLogin() {

                var isLogin = $("#IsLogin").val();
                
                if (isLogin == 1) {
                    $(".OrdersList").css({"display":"none"});
                    $(".Settle").css({"display":"none"});
                    QuickLoginMethod();
                }
                else
                {
                    $(".OrdersList").css({"display":"block"});
                    $(".Settle").css({"display":"block"});
                }
            }
        });
        //快捷登陆
        function CodeCickLogin(objid) {
            objid.src = '/CommonAshx/GenerateValImge.ashx?flag=' + new Date();
            document.getElementById("PicCode").value = "";
            document.getElementById("PicCode").focus();
        }
    </script>

        function setHomePage() {
            if (document.all) {
                document.body.style.behavior = 'url(#default#homepage)';
                document.body.setHomePage("http://www.cx580.com");
            } else if (window.sidebar) {
                if (window.netscape) {
                    try {
                        window.netscape.security.PrivilegeManager
                            .enablePrivilege("UniversalXPConnect");
                    } catch (e) {
                        alert("此操作被游览器拒绝！");
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    <script src="/Web/scripts/zebra_dialog.js" type="text/javascript"></script>

    <script language="javascript">
        $(function () {

            // 判断浏览器是否支持 placeholder
            placeholderLoad();

            function placeholderLoad() {
                if (!placeholderSupport()) {
                    $('[placeholder]').focus(function () {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.val('');
                            input.removeClass('placeholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function () {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.addClass('placeholder');
                            input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
                        }
                    }).blur();
                }
                ;
            }

            function placeholderSupport() {
                return 'placeholder' in document.createElement('input');
            }
        });

        $(function () {
            
            $(".chosen-select").chosen({ disable_search_threshold: 100 });
            $(".QueryForm .ForTips").mouseenter(function (e) {
                $("#Tips").fadeIn("fast").show();
            });
            $(".QueryForm .ForTips").mouseleave(function (e) {
                $("#Tips").fadeOut("fast").hide();
            });
            $("#VerificationCode").click(function (e) {
                
                
                if ($("#Phone").val() == "") {
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('手机号不能为空！',
                        {
                            'type': 'error',
                            'title': '错误信息提示框'
                        });
                    return;
                }
                if (!$("#Phone").val().match(/^1\d{10}$/)) {
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('手机号格式错误！',
                        {
                            'type': 'error',
                            'title': '错误信息提示框'
                        });

                    return;
                }

                $.ajax({
                    url: "../Web/SendPhoneCode.ashx",
                    type: "Post",
                    data: { Phone: $("#Phone").val(), Prefix: $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase(), CarNumber: $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase(), CarCode: $('#txtCarCode').val(), CarDrive: $('#txtCarDrive').val(), Owner: '' },
                    async: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function (result) {

                        if (result.success == true) {

                            DelayCodeTime($("#VerificationCode"), 60);
                        
                            $.Zebra_Dialog('验证码已发送，请查收手机短信',
                                {
                                    'type': 'information',
                                    'title': '提示框'
                                });
             
                        }
                        else 
                        {
                        
                        
                            $.Zebra_Dialog(result.errMsg,
                                {
                                    'type': 'error',
                                    'title': '错误信息提示框'
                                });
                            return false;

                        }

                    }
                });
            });
            $(".ManualOrder").hide();
            $("#ManualBtn").click(function (e) {
                ShowManualForm();
            });
            $("#DropDownForm").click(function (e) {
                ShowManualForm();
            });
            $(".OrdersList li:odd").css("background-color", "#e2f2ff"); //改变偶数行背景色
        });
        function ShowManualForm() {
            var disable = $(".ManualOrder").css("display");
            if (disable == "none") {
                $(".ManualOrder").fadeIn("fast").show("fast");
                $("#DropDownForm").removeClass().addClass("up");
            } else {
                $(".ManualOrder").fadeOut("fast").hide("fast");
                $("#DropDownForm").removeClass().addClass("down");
            }
        }
        function DelayCodeTime(o, t) {//o为按钮的对象，t为时间
            if (t == 0) {
                o.removeAttr("disabled");
                o.removeClass("VerificationCodeDisabled").addClass("VerificationCode");
                o.text("获取验证码"); //改变按钮中value的值 
            } else {
                o.attr("disabled", true); //倒计时过程中禁止点击按钮
                o.addClass("VerificationCodeDisabled");
                o.text(t + " 秒"); //改变按钮中value的值 
                t--;
                setTimeout(function() {
                    DelayCodeTime(o, t); //循环调用 
                }, 1000);
            }

        $(function() {
            
            // 判断浏览器是否支持 placeholder
            placeholderLoad();
            function placeholderLoad() {
                if (!placeholderSupport()) { 
                    $('[placeholder]').focus(function() {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.val('');
                            input.removeClass('placeholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function() {
                        var input = $(this);
                        if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                            input.addClass('placeholder');
                            input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
                        }
                    }).blur();
                }; 
            }
            
            function placeholderSupport() {
                return 'placeholder' in document.createElement('input');
            }
            
            //根据对应的参数提示要输入的车架和发动机号长度
            var setCity = function (infor) {
                var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                var carPrefix = inforArray[0];
                var carEngineLen = inforArray[1];
                var carCarcodeLen = inforArray[2];
                var carOwnerLen = inforArray[3];
                var cityId = inforArray[4];
                
                $("#lblViolationCount").text("");
                $("#lblCarNumber").text("");
                $('#txtPrefix').val(carPrefix);
                $('#txtCarNumber').attr('maxLength', 7 - carPrefix.length);
                //$('#txtCarNumber').val('');
                //$('#txtCarDrive').val('');
                //$('#txtCarCode').val('');
                //$('#txtOwner').val('');
                if (carEngineLen > 0) {
                    $('#liCardrive').show();
                    if (carEngineLen == 99) {
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder', "完整发动机号"); 
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('maxLength', 99);     
                    } else {
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder', '发动机号后' + carEngineLen + '位'); 
                        $('#txtCarDrive').attr('maxLength', carEngineLen);
                    }
                } else {
                    $('#liCardrive').hide();
                    $('#txtCarDrive').val('');
                }
                if (carCarcodeLen > 0) {
                    $('#liCarFrame').show();
                    if (carCarcodeLen == 99) {
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder', "完整车架号");
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('maxLength', 99);
                    } else {
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder', '车架号后' + carCarcodeLen + '位');
                        $('#txtCarCode').attr('carCarcodeLen', 99);
                    }
                } else {
                    $('#liCarFrame').hide();
                    $('#txtCarCode').val('');
                }
                //                if (carOwnerLen > 0) {
                //                    $('#liOwner').show();
                //                    if (carOwnerLen == 99) {
                //                        $('#lblCarOwner').text('完整车辆所有人');
                //                        $('#txtOwner').attr('maxLength', 99);
                //                    } else {
                //                        $('#lblCarOwner').text('车辆所有人后' + carOwnerLen + '位');
                //                        $('#txtOwner').attr('maxLength', carOwnerLen);
                //                    }
                //                } else {
                //                    $('#liOwner').hide();
                //                }
                placeholderLoad(); 
            }; 
            
            //初始化城市，车牌号

            function loadsCity() {
                // 先清空
                
                //                if ($("#Code_Hidden").val() == "code") {
                //                    alert("验证码错误！");
                //                } else {
                //                    document.getElementById('Phone_Li').style.display = "none";
                //                    document.getElementById('Code_Li').style.display = "none"; 
                //                }
                $("#City").empty();
                $("#prefix").empty();
                var index = 0;
                var url ;
                var carNumber ;
                var carPrefix ;
                var carCode ;
                var carEngine ;
                var province ;
                var city ;
                var phone;
                var code;
                if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                    url = $.url($.cookie('carCookie'));
                    carNumber = url.param('carNumber');
                    carPrefix = url.param('carPrefix');
                    carCode = url.param('carCode');
                    carEngine = url.param("carEngine");
                    province = url.param("province");
                    city = url.param("city");
                    phone = url.param("phone");
                    code = url.param("code");
                    $("#Province").val(province);
                    $("#Province").trigger("chosen:updated");
                } else {
                    var id = $("#txtProvince").val();
                    
                    if (id != "") {
                        $("#Province").val(id);
                        $("#Province").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    }
                    
                }
                for (var i = 0; i < InputsCondition.length; i++) {

                    var provinceId = $("#Province").val();
                    
                    if (InputsCondition[i].ProvinceID == provinceId) {
                      
                        for (var j = 0; j < InputsCondition[i].Cities.length; j++) {
                            
                            var citieName = '';
                            if (InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name.length > 5) {
                                citieName = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name.substring(0, 5);
                            } else {
                                citieName = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name;
                            }

                            var option = '<option  tag=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name + ' title=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + ' infor=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + ' proxyEnable=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].ProxyEnable + ' value=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + '>' + citieName + '</option>';
                            $("#City").append(option);
                            var prefixOption = '<option  tag=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].Name + ' title=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + ' infor=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID + ' proxyEnable=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].ProxyEnable + ' value=' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '>'+InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix+'</option>';
                            $("#prefix").append(prefixOption);
                            if (index == 0) {
                                var infor = InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarNumberPrefix + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarEngineLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarCodeLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CarOwnerLen + '*' + InputsCondition[i].Cities[j].CityID;
                                setCity(infor);
                            }
                            index++;

                        }
                    }
                }
                
                $("#City").trigger("chosen:updated");
                $("#prefix").trigger("chosen:updated");
                
                if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                    
                    $("#City").val(city);
                    $("#prefix").val(carPrefix);
                    $("#City").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    $("#prefix").trigger("chosen:updated");
                    $('#txtCarNumber').val(carNumber.replace(carPrefix, '').toUpperCase());
                    $('#txtCarCode').val(carCode);
                    $('#txtCarDrive').val(carEngine);
                    $('#Phone').val(phone);
                }
                $('#txtPrefix').val($("#prefix").val());
                $("#txtProvince").val($("#Province").val());
                $("#txtCity").val($("#City").val());

            // chkAll全选事件
            $("#chkAll").bind("click", function () {
               
                if (document.getElementById("chkAll").checked) {

                       
                    var i = 0;
                    $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                        
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        if (inforArray[2] == '1') {
                            $(this).prop("checked", true);
                            i++;
                        }
                             
                    });
                    if (i == 0) {
                        $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
