                    allCheckbox();
                    
                } else {
                    $("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                    $("[name = chkAlls]:checkbox").prop('checked',false);
                    allCheckbox();
                }

            });
            
            // chkAll全选事件
            $("#chkAlls").bind("click", function () {
                
                if (document.getElementById("chkAlls").checked) {
                    
                    var i = 0;
                    $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                        
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        if (inforArray[2] == '1') {
                            $(this).prop("checked", true);
                            i++;
                        }
                             
                    });
                    if (i == 0) {
                        $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                        return;
                    }
                    //$("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop('checked',true);
                    $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop('checked',true);
                    allCheckbox();
                    
                } else {
                    $("[name = chkItem]:checkbox").prop("checked", false);
                    $("[name = chkAll]:checkbox").prop('checked',false);
                    allCheckbox();
                }

            });
            
            //            $("#chkItem").bind("click", function () {

            //                allCheckbox();

            //            });

            var allCheckbox = function() {
                var sum = 0;
                var amount = 0;
                $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                    
                    if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                        var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                        var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                        amount += parseFloat(inforArray[1]) + parseFloat(inforArray[3]);
                        sum++;

                    }
                });
                $("#Sum").html(sum); 
                $("#Amount").html(amount+".00");
            };

            

        });
        

        function checkInputsConditon () {
            var MinLen = 5;
            var carPrefix = $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
            var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
            var carCode = '';
            var carEngine = '';
            var carOwner = '';
            var $carCode = $('#txtCarCode');
            var $carEngine = $('#txtCarDrive');
            //var $carOwner = $('#txtOwner');
            

            if ($carCode.length > 0 && $('#txtCarCode').attr('placeholder')!=$carCode.val())
                carCode = $carCode.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            if ($carEngine.length > 0 && $('#txtCarDrive').attr('placeholder')!=$carEngine.val())
                carEngine = $carEngine.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            //                if ($carOwner.length > 0)
            //                    carOwner = $carOwner.val().replace(/undefined/g, '');

            var conditions = $('option[infor ^=' + carPrefix + ']').attr('infor');
            if (conditions.length > 0) {
                var inforArray = conditions.split('*');
                var carEngineLen = inforArray[1] == 99 ? MinLen : inforArray[1];
                var carCarcodeLen = inforArray[2] == 99 ? MinLen : inforArray[2];
                //var carOwnerLen = inforArray[3] == 99 ? 2 : inforArray[3];                                //|| carOwnerLen > carOwner.length
                if (carNumber.length < 7 || carEngineLen > carEngine.length || carCarcodeLen > carCode.length ) {
                    return false;
                } else {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        };
            
        function addCookie () {
            var carPrefix = $('#txtPrefix').val().toUpperCase();//$('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
            var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
            var carCode = $('#txtCarCode').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var carEngine = $('#txtCarDrive').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            //  var carOwner = $('#txtOwner').val();
            var code = '';//$('#Code').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var phone = '';//$('#Phone').val().replace(/undefined/g, '');
            var cookie = '';
            if ($.cookie('carCookie') != null) {
                var url = $.url($.cookie('carCookie'));
                if (url.param('carNumber') == carNumber) {
                    if (url.param('carCode') != null && url.param('carCode').length > carCode) {
                        carCode = url.param('carCode');
                    }
                    if (url.param('carEngine') != null && url.param('carEngine').length > carEngine) {
                        carEngine = url.param('carEngine');
                    }
                    //                    if (url.param('phone') != null) {
                    //                        phone = url.param('phone');
                    //                    }
                }
            }
            phone = phone.replace(/undefined/g, '');
            
            //$('#txtPrefix').val($("#prefix").val());
            //    $("#txtProvince").val($("#Province").val());
            //    $("#txtCity").val($("#City").val());    
            var province = $("#txtProvince").val();// $('#Province').val();
            var city = $("#txtCity").val();// $('#City').val();
            var cookieInfor = "?carPrefix=" + carPrefix + "&carNumber=" + carNumber + "&carCode=" + carCode + "&carEngine=" + carEngine + "&phone=" + phone + "&province=" + province + "&city=" + city+"&code="+code;
            // 方便读取参数,直接采用网站链接的形式 无其它特殊意义
            cookie = "http://www.cx580.com" + cookieInfor;
            //            cookie = cookie.replace(/undefined/g, '');
            $.cookie('carCookie', cookie, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
        };

        function submitBtn() {            
            if (checkInputsConditon()) {
                addCookie();
                //location.reload();
                window.location.href = '../Web/Query.aspx?action=queryPageBtn';
                return true;
            } else {
                $.Zebra_Dialog('您好！您输入的信息不符合要求，请按提示信息重新输入！',
                       {
                           'type': 'error',
                           'title': '错误信息提示框'
                       });
                return false;
            }
        };

        function onClickChk() {
            var sum = 0;
            var amount = 0;
            $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                    
                if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                    var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                    var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                    amount += parseFloat(inforArray[1]) + parseFloat(inforArray[3]);
                    sum++;

                }
            });
            $("#Sum").html(sum); 
            $("#Amount").html(amount+".00"); 
        }

        function CreateOrdersBtn() {               
            var id="";
            $("[name='chkItem']").each(function() {
                if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                    var infor = $(this).attr("chkInfor");
                    var inforArray = infor.split('*');
                    id += inforArray[0]+"*";
                }
            });
            if (id == "") {
                alert("请选择违章");
                return false;
            } else {
                
                var response = $.ajax({
                    url: "/CommonAshx/CheckLogin.ashx",
                    type: "POST",
                    async: false
                }).responseText;
                var data = jQuery.parseJSON(response);
                if (data.login) {
                    
                    id = id.substring(0, id.length - 1);
                    var carPrefix = $('#prefix').val().toUpperCase();
                    var carNumber = carPrefix + $('#txtCarNumber').val().toUpperCase();
                    var carCode = $('#txtCarCode').val();
                    var carDrive = $('#txtCarDrive').val();
                    
                    $.Zebra_Dialog('正在下单请稍后......',
                        {
                            'type': 'information',
                            'title': '提示框',
                            'buttons': ['关闭']
                        });

                    $.ajax({
                        url: "/Web/Admin/CreateOrder.ashx",
                        type: "Post",
                        data: { ids:id, carNumber: carNumber, carCode: carCode, carDrive: carDrive},
                        async: false,
                        dataType: "json",
                        success: function (result) {
                            if (result.status == "true") {
                                //
                                //                                $.Zebra_Dialog('创建订单成功！',
                                //                                    {
                                //                                        'type': 'information',
                                //                                        'title': '提示框',
                                //                                        'buttons': ['关闭']
                                //                                    
                                //                                    });
                                window.location = '/Web/Admin/Pay.aspx?Id=' + result.errorMsg;
                            }
                            else {
                                //                                $.Zebra_Dialog(result.errorMsg,
                                //                                    {
                                //                                        'type': 'error',
                                //                                        'title': '错误信息提示框',
                                //                                        'buttons':  ['关闭'],
                                //                                        'onClose':  function() {
                                //                                            this.close();
                                //                                        }
                                //                                    });

                                //                                window.location = '/Web/Query.aspx';
								$(".ZebraDialogOverlay").remove();
                                $(".ZebraDialog").remove();
                                alert(result.errorMsg);
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    });

                } else {
                    QuickLoginMethod();
                }                      
            }    
        };
    </script>

    <script>
        $(function () {
            //IsLogin();
            function IsLogin() {

                var isLogin = $("#IsLogin").val();
                
                if (isLogin == 1) {
                    $(".OrdersList").css({"display":"none"});
                    $(".Settle").css({"display":"none"});
                    QuickLoginMethod();
                }
                else
                {
                    $(".OrdersList").css({"display":"block"});
                    $(".Settle").css({"display":"block"});
                }
            }
        });
        //快捷登陆
        function CodeCickLogin(objid) {
            objid.src = '/CommonAshx/GenerateValImge.ashx?flag=' + new Date();
            document.getElementById("PicCode").value = "";
            document.getElementById("PicCode").focus();
        }
    </script>
